style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">在 H1 和 H2 子标题中使用关键字</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">这向谷歌强调，您的页面专注于该关键字和主题。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">使用关键字丰富的图像文件名和 Alt 文本</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">优化图像不是非常重要，但它可以帮助你获得图片排名和流量。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">添加内部链接</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">内部链接可以帮助 Google 查找、爬取和索引网站上的更多页面（并帮助他们在搜索结果中排名更高）。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">使用同义词和相关术语</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">在具体内容页面，也可以加入同义词和其他关联的词。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">编写诱人的描述</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">虽然在元描述中使用关键字不再是排名因素。当 Google 的搜索者在有机搜索结果中看到引人注目的元描述时，他们更有可能点击您的网站。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">完善移动设备体验</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">现在Google的规则，移动端优先索引，所以所有网站必须有一个比较良好的移动端体验。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><h4><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);font-size:20px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">5. 链接扩展</strong></span></span></h4><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">链接构建是任何谷歌 SEO优化 策略中最难（也是最重要的）部分。</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">一个简单的事实是：如果你的网站没有指向它的后联链接，你可能不会排名很好。通过外展和社交媒体宣传您的内容也很重要。这部分比较复杂，对于外贸人需要了解基础概念即可。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">谷歌官方是不允许做外链的。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">谷歌不建议，认为是违反了Google的网站站长指南。</span></span><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">网站站长指南，可以点击：</span></span><a style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:none;" href="https://vps123.icu/154.html" target="_blank"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,255);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">谷歌初学者指南</span></span></a></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><a style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:none;" href="https://www.globalsir.com/how-to-seo/" target="_blank"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">1. 花钱购买链接或者包含链接的帖子</span></span></a></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">2. 用商品或fuwu服务交换链接</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">3. 向他人发送“免费”产品，以此作为交换来让这些人撰写包含链接的产品评论。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><h2 style="margin-left:0px;"><a style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:none;" name="六、2022年SEO的变化？"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,255);font-size:24px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">六、谷歌优化的变化？</strong></span></span></a></h2><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">谷歌优化有哪些重要趋势？有哪些行之有效的新策略？我们来谈一谈谷歌优化的新变化，2如何做好谷歌优化？</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">我们从以下几个方面来介绍：</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><h4><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);font-size:20px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">1. 页面体验和核心网页指标优化</strong></span></span></h4><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">页面体验是一组衡量用户和网页进行互动体验的因素，可以用来了解网页本身的信息价值之外的互动状态，包括桌面和移动两种设备。当然也包括核心网页指标。</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">核心网页指标是一组衡量真实用户体验的指标，包括网页的加载性能、互动性和视觉稳定性。还包含其他的搜索衡量因素：HTTPS、移动设备适配、干扰插页式广告。</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">这两项内容，打开Google Search Console，就可以找到：</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;text-align:center;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><picture class="lazy-f p-ritxt" style="box-sizing:border-box;float:none;height:0px;width:auto;"><source style="box-sizing:border-box;" type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/623475e2573f9833742391_t_WNo_560d278.webp"><img class="nim scrollLoading" style="box-sizing:border-box;height:auto;opacity:1;transition:0.6s;width:391.393px;" alt="" src="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/623475e2573f9833742391_t_WNo_560d278.png" onload="this.style.opacity=1"></picture></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">根据目前的状态，谷歌会优先惩罚不好的网页，但不一定会提升排名，所以我们要优先处理好已经提示错误的网页。</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">同时根据Google提示，不但优化核心网页指标，比如这个网站优化后数据全面提升。</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><picture class="lazy-f p-ritxt" style="box-sizing:border-box;float:none;height:0px;width:auto;"><source style="box-sizing:border-box;" type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/62347603bca63270085604_t_WNo_1107d713.webp"><img class="nim scrollLoading" style="box-sizing:border-box;height:auto;opacity:1;transition:0.6s;width:782.786px;" alt="" src="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/62347603bca63270085604_t_WNo_1107d713.png" onload="this.style.opacity=1"></picture></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><h4><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);font-size:20px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">2. 谷歌段落排名优化</strong></span></span></h4><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">2020年Google就宣布了一项“Passages”的排名新技术。这项技术，可以让Google对页面的特定段落进行排名。</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">Google不会只考虑整个页面相关性，还会考虑单个段落的相关性。</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">每个段落可以参与排名的机会越来越多。</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;text-align:center;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><picture class="lazy-f p-ritxt" style="box-sizing:border-box;float:none;height:0px;width:auto;"><source style="box-sizing:border-box;" type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/6234761c087bc682294643_t_WNo_682d468.webp"><img class="nim scrollLoading" style="box-sizing:border-box;height:auto;opacity:1;transition:0.6s;width:626.223px;" alt="" src="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/6234761c087bc682294643_t_WNo_682d468.png" onload="this.style.opacity=1"></picture></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">在做内容布局的时候，可以讲内容离散为不同的组成部分。</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;text-align:center;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><picture class="lazy-f p-ritxt" style="box-sizing:border-box;float:none;height:0px;width:auto;"><source style="box-sizing:border-box;" type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/623476357688c932648775_t_WNo_647d754.webp"><img class="nim scrollLoading" style="box-sizing:border-box;height:auto;opacity:1;transition:0.6s;width:626.223px;" alt="" src="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/623476357688c932648775_t_WNo_647d754.png" onload="this.style.opacity=1"></picture></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><h4><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);font-size:20px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">3. 精选摘要优化</strong></span></span></h4><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">精选片段摘要，也就是大家说的“第0位”，这是Google最推崇的内容。</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;text-align:center;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><picture class="lazy-f p-ritxt" style="box-sizing:border-box;float:none;height:0px;width:auto;"><source style="box-sizing:border-box;" type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/62347667b654d952228170_t_WNo_592d273.webp"><img class="nim scrollLoading" style="box-sizing:border-box;height:auto;opacity:1;transition:0.6s;width:547.946px;" alt="" src="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/62347667b654d952228170_t_WNo_592d273.png" onload="this.style.opacity=1"></picture></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><h4><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);font-size:20px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">4. 搜索意图优化</strong></span></span></h4><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">搜索意图是最近一直都在谈论的话题，一般来说，不满足搜索意图的内容根本不会有排名。随着谷歌越来越了解用户的搜索意图，创造满足用户搜索意图的内容显的尤为重要。</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">比如搜索：golf</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">搜索该关键词的人，想了解一些媒体信息。</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><picture class="lazy-f p-ritxt" style="box-sizing:border-box;float:none;height:0px;width:auto;"><source style="box-sizing:border-box;" type="image/webp" srcset="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/62347783704ee849141022_t_WNo_902d916.webp"><img class="nim scrollLoading" style="box-sizing:border-box;height:auto;opacity:1;transition:0.6s;width:782.786px;" alt="" src="https://www.globalsir.com/uploads/62347783704ee849141022_t_WNo_902d916.png" onload="this.style.opacity=1"></picture></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">因此，各位外贸人要针对自己的产品和具体的关键词，创造满足用户搜索意图的内容。</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</div><h4><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);font-size:20px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">5. 视频优化</strong></span></span></h4><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">当视频在Google中越来越重要了。在线视频在2022年占有所有网络流量的82%。优质的视频内容在Google的搜索结果中会有极大板块的展示区</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:16px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">了解 2024 年 Google SEO 新的变化可以访问：</span></span><a style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:none;" href="https://www.globalsir.com/how-to-seo-starter-edition/#:~:text=2023%20Google%20SEO%E4%BC%98%E5%8C%96%E7%9A%84%E6%96%B0%E8%B6%8B%E5%8A%BF" target="_blank"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:16px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">2024谷歌 SEO 新变化</span></span></a></div></div><h3 style="margin-left:0px;">&nbsp;</h3><h2 style="margin-left:0px;"><a style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:none;" name="七、SEO优化中200个常见的谷歌排名规则"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,255);font-size:24px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">七、谷歌优化中200个常见的谷歌排名规则</strong></span></span></a></h2><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">Google规则有很多很多条，而且Google大脑不断的进行规则调整，增加新的因素，调节不同因素的系数等等。</strong>我们vps123把常见的<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">Google SEO优化排名</strong>规则分享给外贸人：</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">1、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">域名年龄</strong>，Google使用域名年龄可以作为一种因素考虑。域名年龄越长一般会增加网站权重。关于如何选择域名，可以看：</span></span><a style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:none;" href="https://vps123.icu/412.html" target="_blank"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,255);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">外贸网站如何选取一个好域名？</span></span></a></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">2、域名中出现关键词不像过去有助于提升排名，但域名中的关键词仍可以作为相关性的一种信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">3、域名开头包含目标关键词在域名开头包含目标关键词，相对于不含关键词或尾部包含关键词的域名有优势。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">4、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">域名的续费时长和到期时间</strong>，暗示Google确实会研究域名注册和更新日期。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">5、子域名使用关键词有可能可以提升排名。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">6、域名历史如果域名所有权多次更迭，那Google可能会重置网站的历史记录，以前域名的反向链接价值会被丢掉。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">7、完全匹配域名如果域名和关键词完全一致，如果网站质量很高，这依然是优势。否则反而更容易被识别惩罚。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">8、公开与隐藏Whois信息。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">9、惩罚网站所有者，如果某人被识别为垃圾邮件发送者，那Google会仔细检查该人拥有的网站是否有意义。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">10、国家专属域名使用国际/地区专属顶级域名（.cn、.ｅｓ等）可以提升在这些国家和地区的排名，但限制了网站在全球获得排名的能力。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">11、标题中包含关键词标题是第二重要的页面因素（除页面内容之外），在页面SEO优化中作用巨大。还有Meta Description中出现关键词也是高相关性的信号，现在不是特别重要，但依然有些用。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">14、H1标签中出现关键词，H1标签是”第二个标题标签“，也非常重要。H1标签作用比P标签对排名的影响大。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">15、页面中出现关键词页面中有关键词比其他任何相关性都更有说服力。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">16、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">内容长度长一般会包含更多关键词</strong>，涵盖的内容也会更广泛，与短小精悍的文章比有优势。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">17、关键词密度虽然不像以前那么重要，但依然会被Google用来确定网页主题。但关键词密度过大会有反作用。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">18、内容中的潜在语义索引关键词（LSI）潜在语义索引关键词（Latent Semantic Indexing = LSI）帮助搜索引擎从多义词中提取具体意义（比如 Apple 识别为苹果公司还是苹果这个水果），所以页面中出现的其他相关词很重要。是否存在LSI词可能作为内容质量的评判标准。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">19、Title和Meta Description中的潜在索引关键词与网页内容一样，Meta标签中的潜在索引关键词（LSI）有助于Google辨别同义词，也可以作为页面相关性信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">20、页面加载速度无论Google还是Bing都使用页面加载速度作为一个排名因素。搜索引擎蜘蛛会根据页面代码和文件大小估算网站速度。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">21、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">重复内容同一网站上的相同内容（可能稍作修改）可能会对网站搜索引擎的收录和排名有负面影响。</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">22、rel=”canonical”标记合理使用 rel=”canonical”标记，会防止Google误判网站内容重复而惩罚。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">23、Chrome浏览器访问速度Google可能会使用Chrome的用户数据来识别与HTML代码无关的页面加载速度情况。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">24、图像优化图片的文件名、Alt文本、Title、Description和Caption都是重要的页面相关性指标。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">25、内容更新速度Google Caffeine算法对时间敏感的搜索很重视，表现就是搜索结果会显示内容更新时间。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">26、内容更新幅度编辑和更新也是一个页面新鲜度因素。添加或删除整个段落才算重要更新，不能只是调换一些词的顺序。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">27、页面历史更新频次页面多久更新?每天、每周、每隔5年?页面更新频率在提升页面新鲜度中起到重要作用。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">28、关键词突出显示关键词出现在页面前100个字中似乎是一个重要的相关信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">29、H2/H3标签中出现关键词将关键词显示在H2或H3标签的副标题中是另一个弱相关信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">30、关键字匹配关键词全字匹配更重要，比如搜索“cat shaving techniques（给猫剃毛技术）”，针对完全匹配做的优化页面就比“techniques for shaving a cat”要好，虽然意思一样。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">31、出站链接质量许多SEO认为链接指向权重网站有助于向Google发送信任信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">32、出站链接主题根据http://Moz.com的试验，搜索引擎可以使用你链接指向的页面作为相关性信号。例如：你有一个汽车相关的页面链接指向了一个电影相关的页面，这可能会告诉Google你的页面是关于汽车电影的，而不只是单指“汽车”。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">33、语法和拼写正确的语法和拼写是一个页面质量信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">34、复制内容页面上的内容是否是原创?如果是从Google索引页面中采集或复制的，它不会获得和原始内容一样的排名。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">35、有用的补充内容根据Google公布的评分指南文件，有用的补充内容是网页质量的指标（也是排名指标），比如货币换算器、贷款利息计算器等。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">36、出站链接数过多的Dofollow出站链接会导致PageRank“泄露”，这会影响到页面的排名。（Google已经取消很久了，但这条规则应该还适用的）</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">37、多媒体图像，视频和其他多媒体元素可以作为内容质量信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">38、指向页面的内部链接的数量网站内链数量表明它相对于其他页面的重要性，越多越重要。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">39、指向页面的内部链接的质量网站里高权重页面的内链效果比低权重（或无权重）的效果好很多。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">40、死链数量页面太多，死链是网站被遗弃或没人维护的特征，Google会使用死链来评估网站首页质量。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">41、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">内容可阅读等级Google会评估网页的阅读难度。</strong>但这条规则有争议，有人认为容易阅读的浅显内容有助于吸引读者，还能提升排名，而有些人则认为容易被认为是内容工厂，随意发布。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">42、联盟链接（Affiliate Link）本身可能不会影响排名。但如果太多的话，Google的算法可能会更加注意你网站的其他质量信号，以确保网站不是一个单薄的联盟链接网站。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">43、HTML错误和W3C验证网站页面很多HTML错误可能是质量差的特征。虽然这点有争议，但很多人依然认为，网页不能通过W3C验证是一种网站质量差的信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">44、网页所在域名权重如果其他一切条件相同，权重高的域名页面排名更好。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">45、页面PageRank虽然并不完全相关，但是一般来说，页面有更高的PR值，排名会比PR值低的好。（Google现在已经没有PR值了，只有Ｍｏｚ自己做了这个工具）</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">46、网址长度URL过长可能会影响搜索排名。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">47、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">URL路径目录层级越浅，越靠近根域名，可以增加URL权重。</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">48、人工干预编辑虽然未得到证实，但Google提交过一项允许人工编辑影响搜索引擎结果页（SERP）的系统专利。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">49、页面类别页面出现在什么类别是一个相关信号，如果页面和类别不相关，则很难获得好的排名。（信息要发布到正确的分类）</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">50、WordPress标签标签是WordPress特定的相关信号。改善搜索引擎优化效果的唯一方法是将一个内容与另一个内容相关联，更具体地说是将一组内容相互关联。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">53、参考资料和来源引用参考资料和来源，如学术论文，可能是高质量内容的标志。Google质量指南规定，引用页面时应注意来源：“是否是专业知识或权威来源，这很很重要”。不过，Google否认他们使用外部链接作为排名因素。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">58、页面年龄虽然Google喜欢新鲜的内容，但是定期更新的旧页面可能会超过新页面。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">59、用户友好的布局，Google的建议“高质量的页面布局会让页面主体部分很容易被用户看到”。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">60、2011年12月的Google更新降低了停靠域名的搜索可见性。（可自行百度：停靠域名）</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">61、创建有用的内容，Google可能会区分“高质量”和“有用的”内容的不同。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">62、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">内容可以提供价值和独特的见解</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">63、联系我们，Google质量文件指出，他们更喜欢具有“适当联系信息”的网站。如果网站的联系信息和whois信息一致，可能会有奖励。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">64、域名信任度，域名获得多少来自种子站点（搜索引擎极度青睐的抓取起始站点）的链接是一个非常重要的排名因素。）</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">65、网站架构一个很好的整合网站架构可以帮助Google识别和抓取、组织你的内容。仓筒结构的理解就是把同一类内容放到不同的目录下，就像农民会把小麦、大麦、燕麦放到独立的仓库，如果混在一起，只能称之为”谷物“，反而降低了价值。结构要点：将同类型和主题的页面放在一起;分离不相关的页面;加强每个目录的着陆页。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">66、网站更新网站的更新频次，尤其是添加新内容时。这是一个很好的提升网站新鲜度的信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">67、页数网站页面数对权重略有影响。至少一个拥有很多内容的大型网站比内容薄弱的赚联盟费网站要强。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">68、站点地图站点地图有助于搜索引擎更轻松、更彻底地抓取和索引你的页面，提高页面可见性（搜索排名）。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">69、网站正常运行时间网站经常维护或宕机可能会影响排名（如果没有及时修复，甚至可能导致减少索引量）</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">70、服务器位置服务器位置可能会影响网站在不同地区的排名，对于地域相关的搜索特别重要。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">71、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">SSL证书已经确认Google会索引SSL证书</strong>，并使用HTTPS作为排名信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">72、服务条款和隐私页面这两个页面有助于告诉Google你的网站是值得信赖的。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">73、重复的Meta标签内容网站页面使用重复一样的Meta keywords和Description可能会降低你的所有页面可见性。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">74、面包屑导航，拥有面包屑导航是用户体验良好的网站结构风格，可以帮助用户（和搜索引擎）知道他们在网站上的位置。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">75、移动版优化，谷歌的官方建议是创建一个响应式网站。响应式网站可能会在移动搜索中获得优势。Google还会对移动搜索结果中没有移动版的页面进行降权。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">76、YouTube优化可能因为Youtube是Google旗下产品，搜索结果页面（SERP）中有特殊排名待遇（排名很好），尤其是Google 熊猫算法后，Youtube流量增加显著。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">77、网站可用性，难用的网站一般用户停留时间短、访问深度浅、跳出率高，这些都会降低排名。这可能是从大量用户数据中收集到的独立算法因素。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">78、Google Analytics（分析）和Google Search Console（网站管理员工具），有些人认为，在网站上安装这两个程序可以改善网页索引。也可能直接影响排名（因为Google可以获得网站更准确的跳出率，是否从反向链接获得流量等）。国内则对应的是百度统计和百度站长工具。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">79、用户评价/网站声誉Yelp.com和RipOffReport.com可能在Google这个算法中发挥了重要作用。Google甚至发布了他们抓住了一个利用用户差评获得反向链接的案例。国内就是百度口碑网站了：百度口碑反向链接因素80、链接的域名年龄老域名的反向链接可能比新域名作用更大。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">81、链接的域名数量，引用域名数量是Google算法中最重要的排名因素之一，另外，链接数是有阈值的，在没有突破阈值前，有可能链接域名越多，排名反而会下降</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">82、独立C类IP的链接数，来自不同C类IP（址的表示范围为：192.0.0.0~223.255.255.255。）数量越多，说明链接广泛性越好。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">83、链接页数链接页面的总数很重要， 即使部分都来自同一个域名，这也对排名有帮助。</span></span></div><div
