style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">84、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">Alt标签（用于图像链接）Alt文本可以说是图像的“锚文本”。</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">85、来自.edu或.gov类域名链接，虽然Google的Matt Cutts说不会做区别对待。但是，这并不妨碍广大SEOer认为Google对.gov和.edu域名的权重算法中有特殊的地方，也就说大家认为来自教育机构和政府网站的链接价值更大。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">86、链接页面的权重反向链接的页面权重（PageRank）是非常重要的排名因素。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">87、链接域名的权重同等页面权重下，域名权重越高越好（PR3站点的PR2页面权重小于PR8网站的PR2页面）。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">88、来自竞争对手的链接如果你能获得关键词搜索结果中其他网站的反向链接，则对于关键词排名特别有价值。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">89、社交网站网站引用页面被社交网站引用可能会影响链接的价值，被引用的越多越好。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">90、来自垃圾网站的链接可能会伤害网站排名。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">91、用户帖子引用，虽然让用户发布引用链接是白帽SEO的一部分，但如果链接来自签名或简介部分，价值可能不如页面内容里的相关链接，尽量能让用户帖子内容里加链接。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">92、来自网站首页的链接权重比内页的要高很多。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">93、Nofollow链接SEO中最有争议的话题之一。Google的官方话是：“一般来说，我们不跟随他们。”这表明他们至少在某些特定情况下会Follow，拥有一定百分比的nofollow链接可用于区分自然与非自然的链接。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">94、链接类型的多样性如果链接都来自某单一来源，比如论坛个人资料和博客评论页面，这明显不自然，会容易识别为垃圾链接。而来自不同来源的链接则是自然链接的标志。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">95、赞助链接，像“合作伙伴”、“赞助商链接”这样的词语可能会降低其附近链接的价值。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">96、内容相关链接页面内容中的链接权（语境链接）重比空白页面（不一定空，比如单独的友情链接页）或其他非价值页面的链接权重更高。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">97、过多301重定向页面根据Google网站管理员帮助视频，过多301重定向链接会稀释部分（甚至全部）PR 。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">98、反向链接锚文本如Google原始算法中说：“首先，锚文本通常能提供比页面本身更准确的网页描述。”锚文本的重要性虽然降低了（可能被Spam利用），但它仍然发送强烈的相关信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">99、内部链接锚文本内部链接锚文本是另一个相关性的信号，虽然可能与反向链接的锚文本权重不同。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">100、链接标题链接标题（当悬停在链接上时出现的文本）也用作弱相关信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">101、引荐域的国家/地区从国家/地区的顶级域名（.de，.cn，co.uk）获取链接可能会帮助网站在该国家排名更好。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">102、内容中的链接位置，在内容开头的链接比内容结尾的链接权重高。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">103、页面中的链接位置通常，在页面主体内容中添加的链接比页面底部或侧边栏中的链接权重更高。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">104、链接域相关性，来自类似主题的垂直网站链接比来自完全不相关网站的链接更强大。有效的SEO策略依然着重于获得相关链接。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">105、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">页面级相关性</strong>，与页面内容紧密相关的链接权重比不相关页面链接权重更高。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">106、链接周围文字代表的情绪，Google可能已经可以根据链接周围文本识别出情绪，分析出链接是推荐还是负面批评引用。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">107、标题中的关键词Google对页面标题中包含对应关键字的链接给予更多权重（“专家链接到专家”，类似于专家间的互相推荐，可信度更高）。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">108、正链接速度，链接增加速度（反向链接增加速度快于减少速度）的网站通常会得到搜索结果排名提升。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">109、负链接速度，链接减少速度（反向链接减少速度快于增加速度）可以显著降低排名，因为它是流行度下降的信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">110、专业主题链接，Aaron Wall声称，从专业的相关主题页面获取的的链接会给予更高的权重。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">111、权威网站链接，从公认的行业权威网站获得的链接比小的专题网站获得好处多。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">112、维基百科的引用链接虽然添加有nofollow标签，但很多人认为，从维基百科获取链接可以让你的网站在搜索引擎眼中增添一点信任和权威。国内可以增加一些来自百度百科和互动百科的引用。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">113、链接附近相关文本，在反向链接周围出现的文本有助于告诉Google你的页面主题。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">114、反向链接添加时间，根据Google专利，以前添加的链接比新加的反向链接具有更多的权重。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">115、真实网站链接，与垃圾博客链接相比，Google给“真实网站”的链接权重比垃圾博客链接高。Google可能会使用品牌和用户互动信号来区分两者。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">116、自然链接，拥有“自然链接”的网站将排名高，而且排名更稳定持久。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">117、互惠链接，Google指出“过度链接交换”是一种作弊，需要避免。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">118、用户生成的内容链接，Google能够识别用户生成（UGC）的链接与实际的网站所有者添加的链接。例如：Google知道来自Wordpress官方博客上的链接与用户创建的wordpress博客joesblog.wordpress.com链接是非常不同的。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">119、来自301跳转的链接，经过301重定向的链接与直接链接相比可能会损失一点点权重，然而Google的Matt Cutts说：301链接类似于直接链接。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">120、Schema.org结构化数据，支持Schema结构化数据的页面可以在Google的搜索结果中出现，从而直接提升搜索结果页的点击率这是不争的事实。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">121、org或gov外部链接，许多人认为，Google会给被org或gov等组织或政府网站链接的网站，给予更多的信任和权重。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">122、链接网站的可信度（TrustRank），网站的可信度也可以传递，如果很多可信度高的网站指向到你网站，对排名有好处。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">123、页面的出站链接数量，页面的PageRank是有限的，导出链接多的页面比导出少的效果差。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">124、来自论坛的链接，由于大量作弊，Google可能会大大降低论坛中链接的权重。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">125、链接页面的字数，1000字帖子中的链接比25个字帖中的链接更有价值。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">126、链接页面的内容质量，拼写错误多，语句不通内容里的链接价值不如专业包含多媒体内容里的链接。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">127、全站链接，Matt Cutts已经确认，全站链接被“压缩”识别为单个链接。用户互动</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">128、搜索关键词的页面点击率，搜索结果中点击率高的页面可能会获得该特定关键字的排名提升。百度算法也是这样，这就是各种“网页快排”技术的理论基础。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">129、所有搜索关键词的页面点击率，所有关键字的网页（或网站）的点击率都是基于人的交互信号，一般都是点击率越高越好。一定要重视优化SERP（搜索结果页），其中页面标题、配图、图标，都是SEO改进的点，以便提升用户的点击率。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">130、跳出率并不是所有SEOer都认同跳出率这个排名因素，但Google很可能会把广大用户作为页面质量测试人员（快速跳出说明页面质量差）。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">131、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">直接流量，已经确认Google使用Google Chrome的数据来确定人们是否访问网站（以及访问频率）</strong>。拥有大量直接流量的网站可能比直接流量少的网站质量更高。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">132、重复流量，Google还可以知道用户是否再次访问这个页面或网站，Google可能会提高再次访问多的网站排名。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">133、被阻止的网站，虽然Google已经在Chrome中停止了这项功能。然而，Google熊猫2.0算法仍然用这个数据作为质量信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">134、Chrome书签，我们知道Google收集Chrome浏览器使用情况数据。被用户加入Chrome书签的页面可能会提升排名。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">135、Google工具栏数据，Danny Goodwin报道Google使用工具栏数据作为排名信号。但是，除了检测页面加载速度和恶意软件之外，不知道Google还从工具栏收集什么数据。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">136、评论数，拥有大量评论的页面是交互好、内容质量高的表现。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">137、停留时间，Google非常注意“停留时间”：Google搜索过来的人在你的页面停留了多长时间。可能是”长点击（点击页面后停留时间长）“，也可能是”短点击（点击页面后停留时间短）“如果人们花费大量时间在你的网站上，Google会认为网站质量很好。特殊算法规则</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">138、搜索结果时效性，对于一些时效性强的搜索（比如突发事件），Google会给新页面更高的权重。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">139、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">搜索结果多样性</strong>，一些模糊搜索词比如“Ted”，“WWF”或“ruby”，Google会给出多样性的搜索结果，因为这些词都用多种含义。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">140、用户浏览历史记录，登录Google账号浏览过的网页，以后搜索相关词时，这个网页会在你的本地搜索结果中有一定的排名提升。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">141、用户搜索历史，你的搜索行为会影响以后的搜索结果。例如：如果你先搜索“评价”，然后搜索“烤面包机”，则Google更有可能在搜索结果中显示”烤面包机评价“。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">142、地理位置定位，Google会优先考虑使用本地服务器IP和国家/地区特定域名的站点。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">143、安全搜索，用户开启安全搜索后，会过滤暴力、色情等非法的搜索结果。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">144、Google+ 圈子，Google对你添加到Google+ 圈子的作者和网站显示更高的结果。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">145、DMCA投诉，Google会降低收到DMCA投诉的页面权重。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">146、搜索结果的域名多样性，谷歌2012年6月4日所谓的“大脚怪更新）”据说在每个SERP页面添加了更多域的页面结果。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">147、交易搜索，Google有时会针对有交易需求的关键字（如航班搜索）显示不同的展示结果。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">148、本地搜索，Google经常将Google plus的本地搜索结果放在“正常”SERP之上。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">149、Google新闻框，某些关键字可以触发Google新闻框样式，比如搜”the beatles（甲壳虫乐队）“。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">150、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">大品牌倾向</strong>，在谷歌2009年的”Vince”算法更新后，开始让大品牌的一些短尾词搜索页面排名提升。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">151、购物结果，Google有时会在SERP中显示Google购物的结果。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">152、图像结果，Google有时会在搜索里显示一些图片搜索结果列表。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">153、搜索彩蛋结果，有些搜索结果会出现彩蛋结果，比如：Google有十几个复活节彩蛋结果。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">154、品牌词结果域名或品牌关键词会显示同一个网站的多个搜索结果。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">155、推文数量和链接一样，包含网址的推文数（twitter提及）可能会影响其在Google的排名。倒是没有听说百度搜索排名与新浪微博提及数的关系。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">156、Twitter用户权重粉丝多，创建早，影响力大的Twitter号比来自新的、低影响力的帐户的推文链接更有影响力。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">157、Facebook Like数量，虽然Google看不到大多数Facebook帐户，但有他们可能把Facebook Like数量当作弱排名信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">158、Facebook分享，Facebook分享与反向链接更相似，应该比Facebook Like数量更有影响力。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">159、Facebook用户权重粉丝多、影响大的Facebook账号上的分享和Like数据，搜索引擎会传达更多权重。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">160、Pinterest收藏，Pinterest是一个很流行的社会化媒体网站，拥有大量的公开资料。Google可能用Pinterest的数据作为排名信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">161、社会化分享，Google可能会用Reddit，Stumbleupon和Digg等网站的分享作为另一种排名信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">162、Google+数量，虽然Matt Cutts明确说过Google+对排名“没有直接影响 ”，但很难相信他们会忽略自己的社交网络。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">163、Google+账号权重，从逻辑上说，Google会更看重权威账号的权重。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">164、Google+认证，作者2013年2月，Google首席执行官埃里克·施密特（Eric Schmidt）声称：“在搜索结果中，已验通过验证的Google+账户排名将高于未验证的账户”尽管Google+作者身份计划已关闭，但Google可能会使用某种形式的身份认证来确定有影响力的在线内容创作者（并提高排名）。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">165、社会信号相关性，Google可能会用分享的内容和链接周围文字判断相关性。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">166、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">网站社交信号</strong>，整站在社交媒体的活跃度信号可能会增加整站的权重，这会有效提高网页的搜索可见性。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">167、品牌名锚文本，品牌名锚文本是一个简单而强大的品牌信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">168、品牌搜索，品牌和品牌组合词搜索的越多，Google对你网站的认可也就越多。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">169、网站Facebook主页和Like，品牌往往拥有Facebook主页，而且Like数很多。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">170、网站Twitter账户和关注者，知名流行品牌的Twitter账户往往有大量关注者。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">171、官方Linkedin页面，大多数真实企业在Linkedin上都有页面。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">172、Linkedin员工标签，Rand Fishkin认为让员工们开通LinkedIn帐号，并在资料中填写公司名称有助于增强公司品牌信号。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">173、合法正常社交，同样拥有10,000关注者的两个社交账户，跟关注者互动多的比少的账户，好很多。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">174、新闻网站的品牌曝光，真正的大品牌能在Google新闻中找到很多相关信息。事实上，一些品牌甚至在搜索结果首页有Google新闻列表。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">175、共同引用品牌在内容中被提及但没有链接指向，Google可能将这种没有链接的品牌提及作为品牌信号。共同引用算法有效降低了外链和锚文本的作用，依然可以识别出某些页面的主题，从而提升关键词排名。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">176、RSS订阅者数，考虑到Google拥有受欢迎的Feedburner RSS服务，他们将RSS订阅数作为人气和品牌信号是有意义的。（现在RSS已经不流行了，不知道Google是否还会使用这个因素）</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">177、Google+ 本地名录，在Google+ 本地名录中找到意味着网站有实体办公室，Google用此来确定你的网站是否为一个大品牌。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">178、网站是否有纳税信息，Moz.com指出Google可能看一个网站是否提供税务信息。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">179、熊猫算法惩罚，很多有低质量内容（特别是内容农场）的网站在被熊猫算法打击后很难在搜索结果中出现。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">180、链接到敏感网站，如果你的网站链接指向到一些敏感网站，像处方药或小额贷款网站，可能会影响你的网站搜索可见性。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">181、重定向，重定向作弊有很大风险。如果被抓住，面临的可能不只是惩罚，甚至是剔除索引，不再收录。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">182、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">弹窗广告或诱导广告Google网站评分指南指出：弹窗广告或诱导广告是低质量网站的标志。</strong></span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">183、网站过度优化，包括很多页面SEO因素，比如关键字堆砌、标题标签堆砌，过度的关键字修饰。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">184、页面过度优化，许多人反映说，企鹅算法不像熊猫算法那样，企鹅算法会针对具体页面（甚至仅针对特定关键字）处理。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">185、首屏广告，“页面布局算法”会对拥有大量广告，而且实际内容很少的网站进行惩罚。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">186、隐藏联盟，广告当试图隐藏联盟链接（特别是隐藏）会带来惩罚。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">187、联盟网站，Google不喜欢联盟广告公司是公开的秘密。许多人认为，通过联盟链接获利的网站会受到Google额外的审查。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">188、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">自动生成内容，Google不喜欢自动生成内容的网站。</strong>如果Google怀疑你的网站靠机器自动生成内容，可能会导致惩罚或剔除索引（俗称拔毛）。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">189、过度操纵PageRank，过度操纵PageRank可能会惩罚，比如把所有出站链接或大部分内链都加上Nofollow。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">190、IP地址进入黑名单，如果你的服务器IP地址被标记黑名单（比如大量发垃圾邮件），可能会影响服务器上的所有网站。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">191、Meta标签作弊，关键词堆砌也可能发生在Meta标记中。如果Google认为你通过Meta标签作弊，那么他们可能会惩罚你的网站。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">192、不自然的导入链接，突然（和不自然）的导入链接增加是虚假链接的特征标志。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">193、企鹅算法惩罚被Google企鹅算法打击的网站，搜索可见性会变差。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">194、低质量链接占比，高黑帽SEO通常使用大量博客评论或论坛链接，很容易识别出作弊。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">195、链接域相关性著名的分析MicroSiteMasters.com发现，Google企鹅算法对大量不自然、不相关网站的链接很敏感，有可能做出惩罚。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">196、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">非自然链接警告</strong>，Google有些时候会通过Google站长工具给站长发警告信，指出发现大量的非自然外链，随后网站的排名会骤降。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">197、链接来自相近的C类IP段网站是不自然的。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">198、<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">“非法”锚文本，大量“非法”锚文本（比如处方药、博彩、小额贷款关键字）指向你的网站，</strong>无论哪种方式，都可能会损害你的网站排名。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">199、人工惩罚广为所知的是Google曾人工惩罚过英国花卉网站Interflora。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">200、出售链接出售链接肯定会影响PageRank，从而伤害到网站的搜索可见性。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">201、Google Sandbox新网站突然获得大量外链，一般会被Google放入Google沙盒中，这会影响网站的搜索可见性。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;,
