sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">202、Google Dance会让排名浮动变化，根据Google专利，这可能是他们检查网站是否试图欺骗算法的一种方式。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">203、Disavow工具使用Google的“链接拒绝工具”可以消除负面SEO受害者网站的人工或算法惩罚。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">204、复议请求，在Google站长工具里提交复议请求，如果成功可以解除惩罚。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">205、临时链接计划Google显然可以识别先创建，然后再快速删除临时链接以避免惩罚的做法，也被称为临时链接方案。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><h3 style="margin-left:0px;"><a style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:none;" name="八、总结"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,255);font-size:24px;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;"><strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">八、总结</strong></span></span></a></h3><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">我们从7个方面，给外贸人介绍了谷歌优化。</span></span></div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">谷歌优化推广是一个系统性的工作，需要对<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">产品知识、网络营销的知识、品牌营销知识、客户需求调研、同行竞争分析等多个方面考虑。</strong></span></span><br>&nbsp;</div><div style="-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;background-color:rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing:border-box;color:rgb(100, 104, 116);font-family:&quot;Noto Sans SC&quot;, sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-weight:300;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-decoration-color:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.75em;">谷歌优化是面向全世界各行各业的，在中国的外贸企业开拓海外市场具有举足轻重的作用。<strong style="box-sizing:border-box;">做好Google的SEO优化推广，同时也要把Google的广告工作做起来，两者结合，更加方便的帮助中国的企业更好的走出去，并且积累属于自己的流量池。</strong></span></span></div>
